namespace = vef_regency

# Setup event for council
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.10000
	title = vef_regency.10000.t
	desc = vef_regency.10000.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	#Should also be triggered by on_new_heir on action

	trigger = {
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { has_dlc = "Rights of Man" }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = regency_decision_run }
		is_emperor = no
		NOT = { has_regency_trigger = yes }
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		NOT = { government = papal_government }
		NOT = { government = bohemian_monarchy }
		NOT = { is_tribal = yes }
		NOT = { is_nomad = yes }
		has_heir = yes
		NOT = { heir_age = 15 }
		NOT = { has_ruler_flag = DLH_regency }
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = regency_decision_run }
	
	option = {	# Led by Queen-mother
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_female = yes }
			NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
		}
		name = "vef_regency.10000.opta"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_opta"
		set_country_flag = queen_regency
	}
	
	option = {	# Led by bureaucrat
		name = "vef_regency.10000.optb"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_optb"
		set_country_flag = bureaucrat_regency
	}
	
	option = {	# Led by uncle
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_1_age value = 1080 }}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_2_age value = 1080 }}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_3_age value = 1080 }}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_4_age value = 1080 }}
			}
		}
		name = "vef_regency.10000.optc"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_optc"
		set_country_flag = uncle_regency
	}
	
	option = {	# Led by noble family
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = aristocratic_privilege value = 25 }}
		name = "vef_regency.10000.optd"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_optd"
		set_country_flag = noble_regency
	}
	
	option = {	# Led by bishop
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion = orthodox
				religion = catholic
				religion = coptic
				religion = nestorian
				religion = anglican
			}
		}
		name = "vef_regency.10000.opte"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_opte"
		set_country_flag = church_regency
	}
	
	option = {	# Led by imam
		trigger = { religion_group = muslim }
		name = "vef_regency.10000.optf"
		custom_tooltip = "vr_10000_optf"
		set_country_flag = church_regency
	}
}

# Heir Ascends the Throne
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.10002
	title = vef_regency.10002.t
	desc = vef_regency.10002.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = vef_regency
		has_heir = yes
		has_regency = no
		heir_age = 15
		is_lesser_in_union = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_regency.10002.opta"
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = no_bohemian_election duration = 30 hidden = yes }
			clr_country_flag = vef_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_1_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_2_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_3_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_4_regency
			kill_ruler = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = HEIR_INHERITS
		#add_stability = 1	#No stab loss on ruler death
	}
}

# Heir Dies During Regency
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.10003
	title = vef_regency.10003.t
	desc = vef_regency.10003.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	#is_triggered_only = yes #on_heir_death
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = vef_regency
		has_heir = no
		government = monarchy
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = queen_leads_regency
				has_country_modifier = noble_leads_regency
			}
		}
		name = "vef_regency.10003.opta"
		add_legitimacy = -20
		clr_country_flag = vef_regency
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_modifier = uncle_leads_regency }
		name = "vef_regency.10003.opta"
		clr_country_flag = vef_regency
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = bureaucrat_leads_regency
				has_country_modifier = church_leads_regency
			}
		}
		name = "vef_regency.10003.opta"
		define_ruler = {}
		add_legitimacy = -30
		clr_country_flag = vef_regency
	}
}

#Clear regency if no longer monarchy
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.10005
	title = vef_regency.10005.t
	desc = vef_regency.10005.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = vef_regency
		NOT = { government = monarchy }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = vef_regency
			clr_country_flag = queen_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_regency
			clr_country_flag = noble_regency
			clr_country_flag = bureaucrat_regency
			clr_country_flag = church_regency
			clr_country_flag = regency_1_inprogress
			clr_country_flag = regency_4_inprogress
			clr_country_flag = uncle_1_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_2_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_3_regency
			clr_country_flag = uncle_4_regency
			
			remove_country_modifier = queen_leads_regency
			remove_country_modifier = bureaucrat_leads_regency
			remove_country_modifier = uncle_leads_regency
			remove_country_modifier = noble_leads_regency
			remove_country_modifier = church_leads_regency
			remove_country_modifier = regent_inquisition
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}	
}


#################
# Random Events #
#################

# Changeup of the council
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.20000
	title = vef_regency.20000.t
	desc = vef_regency.20000.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_regency_trigger = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			17 = { 
				change_adm = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { dip = 1 }
					change_dip = -1 
				}
			}
			17 = { 
				change_adm = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { mil = 1 }
					change_mil = -1 
				}
			}
			17 = { 
				change_dip = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { adm = 1 }
					change_adm = -1 
				}
			}
			16 = { 
				change_dip = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { mil = 1 }
					change_mil = -1 
				}
			}
			16 = { 
				change_mil = 1 
				change_dip = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { adm = 1 }
					change_adm = -1 
				}
			}
			17 = { 
				change_mil = 1 
				if = {
					limit = { dip = 1 }
					change_dip = -1 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_regency.20000.opta"
	}
}

# Uncle takes power
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.20001
	title = vef_regency.20001.t
	desc = vef_regency.20001.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = vef_regency
		has_country_modifier = uncle_leads_regency
		NOT = { government = ottoman_government }
		OR = {	#Will only do this if he has an heir or is young enough to hope he may yet have one
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = uncle_1_regency
				OR = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_1_age value = 480 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen1_1m1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = uncle_2_regency
				OR = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_2_age value = 480 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen1_2m1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = uncle_3_regency
				OR = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_3_age value = 480 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen1_3m1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = uncle_4_regency
				OR = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen0_4_age value = 480 }}
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = male_gen1_4m1_age value = 1080 }}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_regency.20001.opta"
		
		clr_country_flag = vef_regency
		clr_country_flag = regency_effects_applied
		clr_country_flag = regency_decision_run
		remove_country_modifier = uncle_leads_regency
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = uncle_1_regency }
			clr_country_flag = uncle_1_regency
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_gen1_1m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age which = male_gen1_1m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age which = male_gen1_1m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age which = male_gen1_1m4_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age which = female_gen1_1m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age which = female_gen1_1m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age which = female_gen1_1m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age which = female_gen1_1m4_age }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = uncle_2_regency }
			clr_country_flag = uncle_2_regency
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_gen1_2m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age which = male_gen1_2m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age which = male_gen1_2m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age which = male_gen1_2m4_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age which = female_gen1_2m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age which = female_gen1_2m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age which = female_gen1_2m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age which = female_gen1_2m4_age }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = uncle_3_regency }
			clr_country_flag = uncle_3_regency
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_gen1_3m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age which = male_gen1_3m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age which = male_gen1_3m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age which = male_gen1_3m4_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age which = female_gen1_3m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age which = female_gen1_3m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age which = female_gen1_3m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age which = female_gen1_3m4_age }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = uncle_4_regency }
			clr_country_flag = uncle_4_regency
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_1_age which = male_gen1_4m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_2_age which = male_gen1_4m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_3_age which = male_gen1_4m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = male_gen1_4_age which = male_gen1_4m4_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_1_age which = female_gen1_4m1_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_2_age which = female_gen1_4m2_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_3_age which = female_gen1_4m3_age }
			set_variable = { which = female_gen1_4_age which = female_gen1_4m4_age }
		}
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m1_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m2_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m2_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m2_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m3_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m3_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m3_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m4_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m4_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_1m4_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m1_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m2_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m2_sons value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m2_daughters value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m3_age value = 1100 }
		set_variable = { which = male_gen2_2m3_sons value = 0 }

# Inquisition launched
country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.20002
	title = vef_regency.20002.t
	desc = vef_regency.20002.d
	picture = VEF_COURT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = vef_regency
		has_country_modifier = church_leads_regency
		religion = catholic
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "vef_regency.20002.opta"
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = regent_inquisition
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = vef_regency.90000
	title = vef_regency.90000.t
	desc = vef_regency.90000.d

	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { has_country_flag = vef_regency }
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = regency_requirement value = 1.1 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_core_war value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_claim_war value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_trade_war value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_religious_war value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_ally_war value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = regency_colonial_war value = 0 }

			on_trigger = has_country_modifier
			queen_leads_regency = {
				change_variable = { which = regency_ally_war value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = regency_core_war value = 1 }
			}
			uncle_leads_regency = {
				change_variable = { which = regency_core_war value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = regency_claim_war value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = regency_rival_war value = 1 }
			}

				change_variable = { which = regency_trade_war value = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = regency_core_war value = 1 }

		name = "vef_regency.90000.opta"
	}
}
